msg:Stayed for four nights during May Day. The hotel is very close to the subway station. It is convenient to travel and the service is also very good. Whether it is the front desk or the room service, everyone is very friendly. I left the electronic watch and hat when I left the store. I called the hotel. Help us mail it home, here is a special thanks to Ms. Zhao Yanhong from the room depar**ent. The shortcomings of the hotel include flaws in the hardware. When I checked in on April 28, there was no air conditioner. It was said that it would only be available after May Day. No matter how the air conditioner was set, it would blow out hot air. The room depar**ent gave a small fan to deal with it For a moment, there was no air conditioning in the last two days, May 1st and 2nd. Beijing is so hot on May Day, it's ridiculous to stay in a hotel and almost die from the heat. There is also the shower room, no matter how you adjust it, the temperature of the water keeps changing after the handle is fixed, and the temperature difference is very large. Other facilities are also old, the TV picture is not clear, and the toiletries are poor. The star rating of Beijing hotels is indeed very watery. How can this hardware be rated as quasi-four stars?
